   jQuery(document).ready(function() {
				// CUSTOM AJAX CONTENT LOADING FUNCTION
				var ajaxRevslider = function(obj) {
				
					// obj.type : Post Type
					// obj.id : ID of Content to Load
					// obj.aspectratio : The Aspect Ratio of the Container / Media
					// obj.selector : The Container Selector where the Content of Ajax will be injected. It is done via the Essential Grid on Return of Content
					
					var content = "";

					data = {};
					
					data.action = 'revslider_ajax_call_front';
					data.client_action = 'get_slider_html';
					data.token = 'fdb09a6b5e';
					data.type = obj.type;
					data.id = obj.id;
					data.aspectratio = obj.aspectratio;
					
					// SYNC AJAX REQUEST
					jQuery.ajax({
						type:"post",
						url:"http://www.autoblog.gr/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
						dataType: 'json',
						data:data,
						async:false,
						success: function(ret, textStatus, XMLHttpRequest) {
							if(ret.success == true)
								content = ret.data;								
						},
						error: function(e) {
							console.log(e);
						}
					});
					
					 // FIRST RETURN THE CONTENT WHEN IT IS LOADED !!
					 return content;						 
				};
				
				// CUSTOM AJAX FUNCTION TO REMOVE THE SLIDER
				var ajaxRemoveRevslider = function(obj) {
					return jQuery(obj.selector+" .rev_slider").revkill();
				};

				// EXTEND THE AJAX CONTENT LOADING TYPES WITH TYPE AND FUNCTION
				var extendessential = setInterval(function() {
					if (jQuery.fn.tpessential != undefined) {
						clearInterval(extendessential);
						if(typeof(jQuery.fn.tpessential.defaults) !== 'undefined') {
							jQuery.fn.tpessential.defaults.ajaxTypes.push({type:"revslider",func:ajaxRevslider,killfunc:ajaxRemoveRevslider,openAnimationSpeed:0.3});   
							// type:  Name of the Post to load via Ajax into the Essential Grid Ajax Container
							// func: the Function Name which is Called once the Item with the Post Type has been clicked
							// killfunc: function to kill in case the Ajax Window going to be removed (before Remove function !
							// openAnimationSpeed: how quick the Ajax Content window should be animated (default is 0.3)
						}
					}
				},30);
			});

           <table border="0" id="X2036" style="display: none; background: transparent;">
            <tbody>
             <tr>
              <td>
               <blockquote>
                <p style="text-align: justify;">
                 <strong>
                  SEAT ENTERS MOBILE GAMING
                  <br/>
                  Tremendous success for SEATs new Cupra Race game
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <p style="text-align: justify;">
                 With more than a quarter of a million downloads in just three weeks, the new SEAT game for the iPhone/iPod touch has established itself as one of the most popular games for this platform. In fact, after only a week it was already on the Top 3 list of the free applications  in all categories.
                </p>
                <p style="text-align: justify;">
                 The game, which is available for free download in the App Store of Apples iTunes, uses a powerful 3D engine that permits a truly dynamic driving experience with the new SEAT Ibiza Cupra. The car can be customized to personal taste at the beginning of the game and then the adventure starts. You can choose between Test Drive, Time Attack and Race mode for different experiences.
                </p>
                <p style="text-align: justify;">
                 SEAT is entering the mobile gaming platforms in an effort to demonstrate the values of the brand: Sporty, Lively and Design Driven. The Cupra Race game delivers on all factors.
                </p>
                <p style="text-align: justify;">
                 In June, 2009, a web application of the Cupra Race game will be released for members of the Club SEAT (www.clubseat.com)  a fast-growing community with more than 170,000 members worldwide. In the summer an exciting new update will be released with more cars, circuits and competition modes. And this is just the start
                </p>
               </blockquote>
              </td>
             </tr>
            </tbody>
           </table>
